## Statements by subsection

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Types of Magic

- In _Sword World_ , there is a power called **magic** that can produce various mysterious effects by chanting words called **runes** and performing certain procedures at the same time. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01161))_
- Some rune masters are fluent in multiple runes. However, this also has some limitations. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01162))_
- However, this also has some limitations. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01162))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Example:

- There are five types of runes in the world of _Sword World_ . This difference in runes is at the same time a difference in the type of magic. The five runes are **high ancient** , **silent spirit** , **holy prayer** , **daemon scream** , and **dragon roar** . Each has a different source of magical power and a completely different procedure (although _holy prayer_ and _daemon scream_ are essentially the same power, the only difference being the nature of the magic). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01164))_
- Suppose we have an adventurer with priest skill level 1 and shaman skill level 2. This adventurer can use 1st level holy magic and 1st-2nd level spirit magic. He cannot use any ancient magic, nor any holy magic of 2nd level or higher, nor any spirit magic of 3rd level or higher. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01165))_
- One, is that some races may not be able to learn some or all of the runes. These are as explained earlier under 1.2: Races (see p. 13) The other, is that you _cannot_ have more than _one each_ of holy, dark, and dragon roar magic at the same time. These types of magic are obtained through belief in _gods_ , _wicked gods_ , and _dragons_ , respectively. A character cannot hold more than _one_ of these beliefs at the same time. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01166))_
- Each has a different source of magical power and a completely different procedure (although _holy prayer_ and _daemon scream_ are essentially the same power, the only difference being the nature of the magic). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01164))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / How to Use Magic

- In addition to these runes, there are two others that, although weak, can still manifest magical power. They are called **common runes** and **spellsongs** , respectively. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01169))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.4.1 Magic Power

- First, adventurers who use magic are given a score called **magic power** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01172))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Rune Masters and Rune Master Skills

- In _Sword World_ , all those who use magic utilizing runes are called **rune masters** . Rune masters are divided into five types according to the type of magic (runes) they use. Namely, Sorcerer uses **ancient magic** Shaman uses **spirit magic** Priest uses **holy magic** Dark priest uses **dark magic** and dragon priest uses **dragon roar magic** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01177))_
- Each corresponds to the skill for which it is named. Those with the _sorcerer skill_ can use _ancient magic_ and are called _sorcerers_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01178))_
- Magic is not omnipotent. It is only possible to achieve a defined and limited set of effects by weaving certain words (in runes), called **spells** . There are several types of spells, each with different effects. Depending on the strength of their effects, spells are divided into _levels_ from _1-10_ . 1st level spells are very rudimentary, while 10th level spells are very powerful. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01179))_
- However, working with higher level (i.e., more advanced) spells requires a high rune master skill. A rune master can use _all_ magic up to _their_ skill level, but _cannot_ use magic of a _higher_ level than their current skill. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01180))_
- For those who have acquired multiple rune master skills, consider the level of spells you can use for each type of magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01181))_
- If you’ve acquired _multiple_ magic skills, consider the magic power of each _separately_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01183))_
- It is only possible to achieve a defined and limited set of effects by weaving certain words (in runes), called **spells** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01179))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Example:

- An adventurer with priest skill level 1, shaman skill level 2, and 13 intelligence (+2 bonus) would have a magic power of _3_ in holy magic and a magic power of _4_ in spirit magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01185))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Filling out the Character Sheet

- On the Character Sheet, there is a _magic_ field. Characters with rune master skills must write their _runes_ , _skill level_ , and _magic power_ in this field. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01187))_
- **==> picture [348 x 407] intentionally omitted <==** _spirit_ in the _runes_ column and _1_ and _3_ (holy prayer), and _2_ and 4 (silent spirit) in the _level_ and _magic power_ columns to the right of them, respectively. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01190))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Procedure for Casting 5.1.4.3 Non-resistible Magic

- The game procedures for using resistible and non-resistible magic are quite different. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01192))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic

- There are two kinds of magic. One is **resistible** . The other is **non-resistible** . Magic that is _resistible_ can be rendered ineffective or less effective if the target chooses to **resist** . _Non-resistible_ magic can be effective regardless of what the target does. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01196))_
- Declare which magic you’re using, then roll 2D. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01197))_
- That's all. If the result is anything other than double ones, the magic takes effect. If it _is_ double ones, then for some reason (the spell was inaccurate, etc.) the magic takes _no_ effect at all. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01198))_
- This distinction will be specified for each spell in the spell lists that follow. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01199))_
- Declare which magic you’re using, then roll 2D. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01197))_
- If it _is_ double ones, then for some reason (the spell was inaccurate, etc.) the magic takes _no_ effect at all. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01198))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Procedure When an 5.1.4.4 Adventurer Casts Resistible Magic on a Monster

- When attempting to cast _resistible_ magic on a monster, the caster must determine whether their opponent can resist it. You must make a success roll using _caster’s magic power_ as the baseline score and the monster’s **mental point resistance** as the target score. If _2D roll + magic power_ is greater than or equal to the monster’s resistance score, the magic will be cast with its full effect. If the resistance score is _not_ met, the magic will _not_ work or will only have a _weak_ effect. If the 2D roll comes up _double ones_ , that means there was some mistake and the magic did _not_ work. Even if the magic doesn’t normally lose its effect when resisted, in this case it is completely nullified. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01201))_
- If the 2D roll comes up _double sixes_ , the magic automatically succeeds and will take its full effect, no matter how high the monster’s mental point resistance (except for when the magic _itself_ has no effect on that monster. In this case, there is no need to roll the dice, and the magic does not take effect). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01202))_
- If the 2D roll comes up _double ones_ , that means there was some mistake and the magic did _not_ work. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01201))_
- If the resistance score is _not_ met, the magic will _not_ work or will only have a _weak_ effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01201))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Example:

- In this case, the adventurer (the player controlling them) must make a success roll. The baseline score is _4_ (magic power) and the target score is _9_ (goblin's mental point resistance). In other words, if the 2D roll is _5 or mor_ e, _Fire Bolt_ will take its full effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01206))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Procedure When a 5.1.4.5 Monster Casts Resistible Magic on an Adventurer

- When a monster casts magic, the procedure is different from when an adventurer casts magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01215))_
- First, in the case of _non-resistible_ magic, a monster can _never_ fail. There is no need to roll the dice, as the magic will _definitely_ take its effect. In the case of _resistible_ magic, the issue is resolved from the perspective of whether the adventurer is able to resist the magic cast by the monster. This is determined by a success roll using the character's _mental power resistance_ , that is, a _mental power resistance roll_ . The target score is a score called the monster’s **magic intensity** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01216))_
- If the adventurer's final score ( _mental power resistance + 2D_ ) is equal to or greater than the monster's _magic intensity_ , the monster's magic will only take an incomplete effect (some magic will take no effect at all). If the adventurer's final score is _less_ than the monster's magic intensity, they will receive the _full_ effect of the magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01217))_
- Also, since this is considered a success roll, it’ll be an _automatic failure_ if the 2D roll is _double ones_ . No matter how high the adventurer's mental power _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01218))_
- **==> picture [344 x 429] intentionally omitted <==** resistance or how low the monster's magic intensity, the magic will take its _full_ effect. Conversely, _double sixes_ is an _automatic success_ , so in this case, regardless of the adventurer's mental power resistance or the monster's magic intensity, that’s a _successful resist_ * and the magic will only take an incomplete effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01219))_
- Conversely, _double sixes_ is an _automatic success_ , so in this case, regardless of the adventurer's mental power resistance or the monster's magic intensity, that’s a _successful resist_ * and the magic will only take an incomplete effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01219))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Example:

- Ducard II (mental power resistance 4) is attacked by a dark elf during an adventure. Dark elves have the ability to use spirit magic, with a magic intensity of 13. If the dark elf casts a _Fire Bolt_ on When the 2D roll is _double ones_ , the resist _automatically fails_ _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01227))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Procedure When an 5.1.4.6 Adventurer Casts Resistible Magic on an Adventurer

- Just like player characters, even those whose data was created for a character may appear as an enemy. If such an enemy casts magic on an adventurer, or if an adventurer casts magic on such an enemy, both sides must roll dice to resolve the situation, just as in weapon combat between adventurers. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01230))_
- In other words, you compare the _magic power + 2D_ score of the one casting the magic with the _mental power resistance + 2D_ score of the one on whom the magic is being cast. If the score of the one casting the magic is greater, the magic will take _full_ effect, but if there is a tie or if the score of the one on whom the magic is being cast is greater, the magic is _resisted_ and will only take an _incomplete_ effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01231))_
- The resolution of _double ones_ and _double sixes_ is also the same as weapon combat. In other words, if the _resisting side_ rolls double sixes, the resist is an _unconditional success_ , otherwise, if _the side casting the magic_ rolls double sixes, the resist is a _failure_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01232))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Handling Resistible Magic 5.1.4.7 and Multiple Targets

- This kind of magic can have multiple targets, and each target must make their own check to resist. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01237))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Example:

- Suppose an adventurer with sorcerer skill level 3 and a +2 intelligence bonus (magic power 5) casts the spell _Lightning_ . _Lightning_ is a spell that shoots a bolt of lightning, dealing damage to everything in its path. If there are multiple targets in the path of the lightning bolt, you must make a check for each one’s attempt to resist. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01244))_
- Suppose there are three goblins (each with a mental point resistance of 9) and one goblin lord (mental point resistance 12) in this space. The player rolls the dice four times and for each one must determine whether the magic breaks through the resist and takes its full effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01248))_
- If the rolls against the three goblins were _6_ , _3_ , and _2_ (double ones!), and the roll against the goblin lord was _6_ , then the result would look like this: _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01250))_
- If the rolls against the three goblins were _6_ , _3_ , and _2_ (double ones!), and the roll against the goblin lord was _6_ , then the result would look like this: _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01250))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.6 Recovering Mental Power / Example:

- A centaur and three adventurers get into a fight. This centaur has the ability to use ancient magic and unleashes _Lightning_ . The game master declares that its magic intensity is _13_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01256))_
- Each of the three adventurers (the players in control) roll 2D to check if they resist, using _their mental power resistance_ as the baseline score, and _13 (magic intensity)_ as the target score. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01257))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.6 Recovering Mental Power / When an Adventurer Casts Magic on Adventurers

- The following procedure is used to make a check when data created for a character casts magic on adventurers, and vice versa. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01259))_
- First, the side casting the magic rolls 2D. The final score (magic power + 2D) must then be determined this one time only. Each resisting side must then make a mental power resistance roll, using that determined final score as the target score. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01260))_
- The final score (magic power + 2D) must then be determined this one time only. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01260))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.6 Recovering Mental Power / Example:

- The evil sorcerer Gorman (magic power 5) unleashes _Lightning_ on the three adventurers. First, Gorman rolls 2D and adds his own magic power. If we assume his 2D roll is _8_ , each of the three adventurers must make a mental power resistance roll, with a target score of 5 (magic power) + 8 (roll) = _13_ . Suppose that the baseline score of all three of their mental power resistance rolls is _4_ . If their rolls are each _2_ (double ones!), _6_ , and _9_ , then only the _last_ one is able to resist the _Lightning_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01262))_
- Handling double ones and double sixes is no different from when there’s only one target. If the side casting the magic rolls double ones, the magic has _no_ effect on _any_ targets. If the side casting the magic rolls double sixes, _no_ _one_ can resist, except for those who _also_ roll double sixes. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01263))_
- If their rolls are each _2_ (double ones!), _6_ , and _9_ , then only the _last_ one is able to resist the _Lightning_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01262))_
- Handling double ones and double sixes is no different from when there’s only one target. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01263))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.6 Recovering Mental Power / Adventurers and Monsters

- Sometimes enemies written in the same data format as a character may also be accompanied by monsters. For example, a sorcerer who leads undead monsters to attack villages. Casting magic on such a group is handled the same way as when an adventurer casts magic on (a group of) adventurers, as described above. At this time, the monsters must _also_ roll the dice to make resist checks. Please use the optional rules under _17.1: Changes to Magic Procedure_ (see p. 273). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01266))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.6 Recovering Mental Power / If the Target Does 5.1.4.8 Not Resist

- Some magic can also have secondary effects. For example, the spirit magic _Fanaticism_ increases attack power, but conversely _decreases_ evasion speed. With such magic, the one on whom it is cast can _choose_ whether or not to resist. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01268))_
- If the one on whom the magic is being cast chooses _not_ to resist the magic, it will _definitely_ take effect so long as the one casting the magic does _not_ roll double ones. You’re also allowed to choose to _not resist_ magic like _Fire Bolt_ , which will definitely result in a loss if it's cast on you....... but that probably won't benefit you in any way. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01269))_
- For example, the spirit magic _Fanaticism_ increases attack power, but conversely _decreases_ evasion speed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01268))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Consuming Mental Power

- Adventurers cannot use magic endlessly. When using magic, an adventurer must temporarily _reduce_ their mental power. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01272))_
- Each magic has a score called **base mental power cost** . This base mental power cost, divided by the corresponding rune master skill level (rounded up), equals the actual mental power consumed by the character. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01273))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Example:

- A character with shaman skill level 2 uses the _Fire Bolt_ spell. The base mental power cost for _Fire Bolt_ is _5_ . The character must consume 5 ÷ 2 = 2.5, rounding up to _3_ points of mental power. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01275))_
- A character can reduce their mental power to 0, but they _cannot_ make it negative. For example, a character with 5 points of mental power remaining _can_ use magic that costs 5 points of mental power, but _cannot_ use magic that costs _6 or more_ points of mental power. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01276))_
- If a character’s mental power reaches _0_ , they will _lose consciousness_ . The character cannot regain consciousness unless they recover their mental power to _1 point or more_ in some way. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01277))_
- For example, a character with 5 points of mental power remaining _can_ use magic that costs 5 points of mental power, but _cannot_ use magic that costs _6 or more_ points of mental power. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01276))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / Recovering Mental Power

- Mental power reduced due to using magic, etc. can be recovered via the following methods. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01281))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 《 Magical Recovery 》

- There's magic and magical items that can recover a character's mental power, such as the holy magic _Transfer Mental Power_ . The amount recovered is explained under each magic and item. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01283))_
- There's magic and magical items that can recover a character's mental power, such as the holy magic _Transfer Mental Power_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01283))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 《 Recovery via Sleep 》

- If a character sleeps for at least 6 hours in a row, they will fully recover their mental power upon awakening. However, this method of recovery can only be done _once_ a day. If you awaken _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01285))_
- However, this method of recovery can only be done _once_ a day. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01285))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion

- within 24 hours of your previous awakening (when your mental power was last recovered), your mental power will _not_ be recovered. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01288))_
- You can increase the effectiveness and certainty of magic by consuming extra mental power. This is called **magic expansion** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01291))_
- Magic expansion is done by doubling or tripling...... the _amount_ of mental power consumed. At this time, you do _not_ double or triple the base mental power cost....... Instead, you divide the mental power by your _skill level, rounded up_ , or in other words, the mental power you would consume when _not_ expanding is doubled, tripled...... etc. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01292))_
- within 24 hours of your previous awakening (when your mental power was last recovered), your mental power will _not_ be recovered. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01288))_
- This is called **magic expansion** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01291))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion / 5.1.7.1 Expansion Types

- Magic expansion includes the following types. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01296))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion / 《 Targets Expansion 》

- If it's _two_ or _three_ targets...... the mental power consumed will also be _doubled_ or _tripled_ ....... _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01299))_
- For spells that can perform this expansion, **targets** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01301))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion / 《 Area Expansion 》

- If the area is _doubled_ or _tripled_ ...... the mental power consumed will also be _doubled_ or _tripled_ ....... You can also expand an area by a _fraction_ (x1.5, x8/3, etc.), in which case the fraction is _rounded up_ when determining the multiplier for mental power consumed. So for expansions such as _x 1.5_ and _x 8/3_ , the cost would be _double_ and _triple_ , respectively. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01304))_
- Since it’s the area that gets expanded, the radius of a circle, a side of a square, etc., can only be increased by the _square root_ of the expansion rate. Please see Table 5-1: Area and Size Expansion. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01305))_
- For spells that can perform this expansion, **area** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01306))_
- So for expansions such as _x 1.5_ and _x 8/3_ , the cost would be _double_ and _triple_ , respectively. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01304))_
- Since it’s the area that gets expanded, the radius of a circle, a side of a square, etc., can only be increased by the _square root_ of the expansion rate. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01305))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion / 《 Volume Expansion 》

- Some spells that affect a space or object can have their volume expanded. If the volume is expanded by _two_ or _three_ times...... the mental power consumed will also be _doubled_ or _tripled_ ....... Rounding should be handled the same way you would for area expansion. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01308))_
- Since it’s the volume that gets expanded, the radius of a sphere, a side of a cube, etc., can only be increased by the _cube root_ of the expansion rate. Please see Table 5-1: Area and Size Expansion. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01309))_
- For spells that can perform this expansion, **target volume** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01310))_
- Note: On the table, _expansion rate_ is the multiplier for mental power consumed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01313))_
- When you cast a spell by consuming that multiplied amount of mental power, multiply the number in _area expansion length_ or _volume expansion length_ by the number (radius, side) that represents the spell’s _area of effect_ , and the result will be the spell’s _area_ . For spells cast on a flat surface, use the number in the _area expansion length_ column, and for spells cast into space, use the number in the _volume expansion length_ column. For example, when you cast the ancient magic _Light_ , whose area is _A space with a 10 meter radius_ , by consuming _double_ the mental power, the resulting area will be a spherical space with a radius of _10 x 1.3 =_ _**13 meters**_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01314))_
- Since it’s the volume that gets expanded, the radius of a sphere, a side of a cube, etc., can only be increased by the _cube root_ of the expansion rate. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01309))_
- For example, when you cast the ancient magic _Light_ , whose area is _A space with a 10 meter radius_ , by consuming _double_ the mental power, the resulting area will be a spherical space with a radius of _10 x 1.3 =_ _**13 meters**_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01314))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion / 《 Duration Expansion 》

- For spells whose effects last a certain amount of time, you can expand that duration. If the duration is _doubled_ or _tripled_ ...... the mental power consumed will also be _doubled_ or _tripled_ ....... You can also increase it by a fraction, such as x1.5, in which case the fraction is _rounded up_ when determining the multiplier for mental power consumed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01316))_
- For spells that can perform this expansion, **duration** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01317))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7 Magic Expansion / 《 Distance Expansion 》

- Magic basically only works up to a certain distance. However, there are spells that can extend their reach. If reach distance is _doubled_ or _tripled_ ...... the mental power consumed will also be _doubled_ or _tripled_ ....... You can also increase it by a fraction, such as x1.5, in which case the fraction is _rounded up_ when determining the multiplier for mental power consumed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01319))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.8 Magic Contraction

- For spells that can perform this expansion, **distance** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01322))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.8 Magic Contraction / 《 Damage Expansion 》

- For spells that deal damage, expansion can increase the certainty of that damage. If you _double_ or _triple_ the amount of mental power you consume...... you can make a damage check (strike roll) _twice_ or _three times_ . The damage you will deal is equal to the _greatest_ of all the strike rolls you made in this way ( _not_ the total). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01324))_
- For spells that can perform this expansion, **damage certainty** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01325))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.8 Magic Contraction / 《 Final Score Increase 》

- There's some magic whose effects are negated or reduced if they're resisted by the target, but will also let you _increase_ the magic's final score (resist target score) in order to prevent this. This increase in final score may also take effect if a nullifying spell is cast later. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01327))_
- For spells that can perform this expansion, **final score** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01329))_
- This expansion requires a deep proficiency in magic. Therefore, it cannot be done infinitely. Final score can only be increased up to a maximum of _caster's rune master skill level ÷ 2 (rounded up)_ . That’s up to _+1 (double)_ for 1st~2nd level, _+2 (triple)_ for 3rd~4th level, and _+5 (sextuple)_ for 9th~10th level. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01330))_
- Therefore, it cannot be done infinitely. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01330))_
- Final score can only be increased up to a maximum of _caster's rune master skill level ÷ 2 (rounded up)_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01330))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.8 Magic Contraction / 《 Effect Expansion 》

- Some expansions don’t fall into any of the above types. For spells that can perform these special expansions, **effect** is written in the _expansion_ section of the magic details, and an explanation is given under each spell. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01332))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1 Basic Rules of Magic / 5.1.7.2 Combined Expansion

- Some magic allows for multiple expansion types. In these cases, you can perform multiple expansions at the same time. However, at this time, the amount of mental power consumed will become extremely large. By multiplying the rates determined for each expansion, you can determine the total multiplied rate of mental power consumed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01334))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / Example:

- Suppose a sorcerer casts an _Energy Bolt_ on three enemies ( _x 3_ expansion) with a +1 to his final score ( _x 2_ expansion) and he makes 4 damage checks for each ( _x 4_ expansion). In this case, the multiplied rate of mental power consumed is 3 x 2 x 4 = **24!** _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01336))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / Magic Contraction

- Magic can also be **contracted** as opposed to expanded. However, this does _not_ reduce the amount of mental power consumed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01339))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 《 Area Contraction 》

- You can make the area of effect narrower than originally intended. The shape (usually a circle) _cannot_ be changed. You also cannot cast it in such a way that it hits the enemy directly in the eyes. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01343))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 《 Volume Contraction 》

- Similar to area contraction, you can also reduce the volume of the targeted object or space. Again, the shape cannot be changed, and you cannot directly aim it at the enemy's eyes. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01345))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 《 Duration Contraction 》

- Magic with a duration can be optionally shortened. However, you _cannot_ set a time that causes the effect to wear off in the middle of a round. You may _only_ set it to wear off at the _end_ of a round. You must also decide how long you want the magic to last _before_ you cast it. Magic that’s already been cast cannot be canceled at will. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01347))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 《 Magic Power Decrease 》

- Magic power can be optionally reduced. This will reduce the final score and, if it's damage magic, _also_ reduce bonus damage (it’s not possible to _only_ reduce the final score or _only_ reduce bonus damage). You must declare how many points you’ll reduce _before_ you roll the dice. If used on multiple targets, you must reduce it by the same amount for _all_ of them. Also, if the side casting the magic rolls double sixes, the resisting side will _also_ need double sixes, no matter _how much_ magic power was declared to be decreased (if it's a monster, it _cannot_ resist). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01349))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 《 Effect Contraction 》

- All magic that can expand their effects can also contract their effects. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01351))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types

- These characteristics are presented here as **magic types** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01359))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Damage 》

- A spell that deals damage to the target's life force or mental power. Spells of the damage type always have a clearly defined _strike power_ . If you manage to break through the target's resist, use the spell's strike power to determine damage by making a _strike roll_ using the Rating Table, same as if you had hit with a weapon in weapon combat. The key number is, of course, the indicated _strike power_ . If you roll 10 or greater during the strike roll, a _critical_ will occur and deal even more damage, same as in weapon combat. Conversely, If you roll double ones, it does _not_ deal any damage at all. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01361))_
- Most magic of the **damage** type can still deal damage even if it's resisted by the target, only with a reduced effect. In this case, you must make the strike roll after _subtracting 10_ from strike power. Also, at this time, no matter how high you roll during your strike roll, a _critical_ will _not_ occur. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01362))_
- In either case, the caster's magic power can be added as bonus damage to the result of the strike roll. Also, the target's adventurer level (or the monster's monster level) is subtracted from the damage. However, there’s an _exception_ if you roll _double ones_ during your strike roll. In this case, no matter how much magic power your character (monster) has, they _cannot_ deal damage to the target at all. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01363))_
- Also, even magic of the _damage_ type may in rare cases take no effect if resisted. At this time, if the target successfully resists, you _cannot_ make a strike roll. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01364))_
- In this case, you must make the strike roll after _subtracting 10_ from strike power. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01362))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Target Score 》

- Some magic can nullify the effects of other magic. For example, the ancient magic _Dispel Magic_ nullifies the effects of most magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01366))_
- Most magic is automatically nullified if a nullifying spell is used, but there are some that are not. This is magic that has a _target score_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01367))_
- When casting any magic, no matter what kind of magic it is, you must roll 2D to check whether an automatic failure (double ones) will occur or not. If you're trying to nullify magic that has a _target score_ with another spell, you must use that other spell's 2D roll to determine your final score. This final score equals _magic power + 2D roll_ (similar to a final score for other success rolls). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01368))_
- If this final score is greater than or equal to the _target score_ originally set for that first magic that was cast, then that first magic can be nullified. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01369))_
- This _target score_ equals the final score of the first magic that was cast (in other words, the magic you're about to nullify). Therefore, when an adventurer uses magic that has a _target score_ , that player should note down that score and remember it. However, if you feel this is cumbersome, or if you forget to make a note, then when it becomes necessary (nullifying magic has been used), you can roll 2D on the spot to determine a final score = _target score_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01370))_
- If this final score is greater than or equal to the _target score_ originally set for that first magic that was cast, then that first magic can be nullified. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01369))_
- Therefore, when an adventurer uses magic that has a _target score_ , that player should note down that score and remember it. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01370))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Counters (Negates) 》

- When magic is cast against other magic, their effects may completely cancel each other out. For example, there are two kinds of ancient magic, _Decrease Weight_ (which makes an object lighter) and _Increase Weight_ (which makes an object heavier), but when both of these are cast on the same object at the same time, they will cancel each other out and disappear without taking effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01374))_
- Such magic, that is, magic that negates the effect of other magic, but at the same time is negated by that other magic without taking its own effect, is called **counters (negates):** type. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01375))_
- When casting _counters (negates):_ magic to cancel the effect of certain magic, if the magic that was cast prior has a _target score_ , then according to the definition of _magic with a target score_ , the magic that's cast after _cannot_ cancel the prior magic unless its final score is greater than or equal to the determined _target score_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01376))_
- For example, there are two kinds of ancient magic, _Decrease Weight_ (which makes an object lighter) and _Increase Weight_ (which makes an object heavier), but when both of these are cast on the same object at the same time, they will cancel each other out and disappear without taking effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01374))_
- Such magic, that is, magic that negates the effect of other magic, but at the same time is negated by that other magic without taking its own effect, is called **counters (negates):** type. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01375))_
- When casting _counters (negates):_ magic to cancel the effect of certain magic, if the magic that was cast prior has a _target score_ , then according to the definition of _magic with a target score_ , the magic that's cast after _cannot_ cancel the prior magic unless its final score is greater than or equal to the determined _target score_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01376))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Counters (Overpowers) 》

- When certain magic is cast against other magic, it can cancel the effect of the prior magic but still take its own effect afterwards. This is magic of the **counters (overpowers):** type. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01378))_
- For example, the ancient magic _Darkness_ can nullify the effects of the spirit magic _Will-O-Wisp_ and still close the surrounding area in darkness, which means _Darkness_ itself is more effective. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01379))_
- However, this is often not automatic. One, is when the target _resists_ . In the case of magic that does not take effect if resisted, if the target _does_ resist it, the magic will _not_ take its effect, and the effect of the _prior_ magic will continue. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01380))_
- The other, is when the prior magic has a _target score_ . In this case, according to the definition of _magic with a target score_ , the magic cast after will _not_ take effect unless its final score is greater than or equal to the determined _target score_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01381))_
- If the magic cast prior has a _target score_ and the magic cast after is _resistible_ , please follow the procedure below to make a check. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01382))_
- ② Next, the one casting the magic must roll 2D to find their final score (by adding their magic power). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01385))_
- ③ Compare _target score in_ ① with _final score in_ ②. If the final score does not reach the target score, the magic will _not_ be cast. This ends here. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01386))_
- ④ If _final score in_ ② is greater than or equal to _target score in_ ①, the target may attempt to _resist_ . The _resist target score_ equals the _final score in_ ②. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01387))_
- ⑤ If the target _successfully resisted_ in ④, the new magic cast will _not_ take effect. The effect of the _prior_ magic will continue. If the target _failed to resist_ , the new magic cast _will_ take effect and the effect of the prior magic will be _negated_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01388))_
- _Counters (overpowers):_ magic does not mean that certain magic is definitely stronger than other magic. It's possible for magic A to _counter (overpower)_ magic B, and at the same time for magic B to _counter (overpower)_ magic A. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01389))_
- Also, all magic _counters (overpowers)_ itself. Therefore, if certain magic takes effect, and you cast that same magic on the same target _multiple_ times, the effect will _not_ be cumulative. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01390))_
- For example, the ancient magic _Darkness_ can nullify the effects of the spirit magic _Will-O-Wisp_ and still close the surrounding area in darkness, which means _Darkness_ itself is more effective. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01379))_
- In this case, according to the definition of _magic with a target score_ , the magic cast after will _not_ take effect unless its final score is greater than or equal to the determined _target score_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01381))_
- If the magic cast prior has a _target score_ and the magic cast after is _resistible_ , please follow the procedure below to make a check. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01382))_
- Therefore, if certain magic takes effect, and you cast that same magic on the same target _multiple_ times, the effect will _not_ be cumulative. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01390))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Mind 》

- This is magic that affects the target's mental state. This kind of magic can only take effect on one target at a time. If magic of the **mind** type is cast on a target, and other magic also of the _mind_ type is cast on that target, the _new_ magic will take effect, and the prior magic will be _nullified_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01392))_
- In other words, all _mind_ magic _counters (overpowers)_ other _mind_ magic. Note that many are _resistible_ magic, and some have _target scores_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01393))_
- This kind of magic can only take effect on one target at a time. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01392))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Physical Ability 》

- This is magic that affects the target’s physical abilities (strength, etc.). Magic of this type can _only_ take effect on _humans_ , _fae_ , and _youma_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01395))_
- Also, with magic of the **physical ability** type, two or more cannot affect the same target at the same time. Please resolve them as _counters (overpowers)_ magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01396))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Weapon Enhancement 》

- Magic that targets a weapon and enhances it. Two or more of this kind of magic cannot affect the same weapon at the same time. Please resolve them as _counters (overpowers)_ magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01399))_
- Weapons that have been given power by ancient magic, silver weapons, or mithril silver weapons are assumed to already have _non-removable_ (see below) **weapon enhancement** magic cast on them. Therefore, that power _cannot_ be nullified, so even if you cast new _weapon enhancement_ magic, it’ll be _useless_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01400))_
- Therefore, that power _cannot_ be nullified, so even if you cast new _weapon enhancement_ magic, it’ll be _useless_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01400))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Non-removable 》

- Some magic, such as _Dispel Magic_ (ancient magic) and _Remove Curse_ (holy magic), can be used as counter magic that _removes_ other magic. However, magic of the **non-removable** type _cannot_ be removed by other magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01402))_
- Although, the ancient magic _Perfect Cancellation_ **is** able to remove _nonremovable_ magic. Also, sometimes there is counter magic that counters _certain_ magic, which if specified, will be removed by _that_ counter magic. It's also possible to remove _non-removable magic_ by directly using the power of a god (wicked god) with the holy/dark magic _Call God_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01403))_
- Some magic, such as _Dispel Magic_ (ancient magic) and _Remove Curse_ (holy magic), can be used as counter magic that _removes_ other magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01402))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Curse 》

- _Dispel Magic_ (ancient magic) can be used to remove most magic, but for magic of the **curse** type, this is not possible. However, _Remove Curse_ (holy magic) **can** be used to remove it. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01405))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Detection 》

- A spell that detects objects, people, magic power, etc. These can be targeted by the ancient magic _Counter Sense_ . These spells also ignore the protection of the ancient magic _Magic Protection_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01407))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.9 Magic Types / 《 Focus 》

- Magic has a fixed _duration_ . Magic of the **focus** type is that in which the magic's effect lasts as long as the caster (the one who casts the magic) is _focused_ . While focusing, the caster cannot take the following actions: _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01409))_
- Attack another with a weapon (or barehanded) Move more than 3 meters in one round _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01411))_
- Even while focusing, if another attacks you with a weapon, etc. you can still attempt to _evade_ it. If magic is cast on you, it's also possible to _resist_ it. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01414))_
- Also, when the target is no longer within the magic's area of effect (out of reach, out of sight, etc.), the magic will _lose_ its effect, even if you continue to focus. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01415))_
- If the caster suffers damage to their life force or mental power, their focus will be interrupted and the magic's effect will be _lost_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01416))_
- If the caster wishes to voluntarily release their focus (in order to take another action), they must declare it at the _beginning_ of the round, when no one else has made their action announcements yet. If your focus is interrupted due to damage, etc. your focus will be interrupted at the timing in which the damage is dealt. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01417))_
- Also, when the target is no longer within the magic's area of effect (out of reach, out of sight, etc.), the magic will _lose_ its effect, even if you continue to focus. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01415))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.10 How to Read Magic Details

- opponent’s sensory organs and give them false sensations. There are three types of senses through which monsters perceive their surroundings: **five senses** , **pseudo** senses, and **magic** senses. Magic of the **illusion** type is effective on those that perceive their surroundings with _five senses_ or _pseudo_ senses. Humans and fae perceive their surroundings through _five senses_ , so they can all be targeted by _illusions_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01422))_
- If the target does not have the senses to deceive, this spell will have no effect at all. It is completely ineffective against monsters who perceive their surroundings through _magic_ senses, and illusions that deceive vision are useless against monsters who _lack_ vision. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01423))_
- The effects of spells of the _illusion_ type can be detected by a resistance roll. However, in order to do this, you must first be suspicious of the illusion. The game master should decide in which cases it seems suspicious. In the case of player characters (adventurers), this may be when the players themselves suspect an illusion. For NPCs and monsters, the game master should decide based on their intelligence. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01424))_
- For example, suppose a fake floor is created above a pit using a _Create Image_ (ancient magic) spell. No matter how smart you are, you’re not likely to notice this. But what if whoever was walking at the front of the line had the misfortune to step on top of it and fall? _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01425))_
- No matter how foolish you are, you should suspect that the floor is an illusion. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01426))_
- It might be unreasonable for a monster with low intelligence, such as a goblin, but a human of average intelligence would find it suspicious. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01428))_
- In the event of such a suspicion, the target of the illusion can make a mental power resistance roll. The target score is the final score from when the illusion spell was cast (if you forgot, roll the dice and determine it again). If you’re successful, you’ll be able to see through the illusion and know the correct situation. However, you can only make this resistance roll _once_ . Once you fail, no matter how suspicious it may be, you won't be able to detect its true form (of course, you _can_ walk around suspicious floors). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01429))_
- For example, suppose a fake floor is created above a pit using a _Create Image_ (ancient magic) spell. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01425))_
- It might be unreasonable for a monster with low intelligence, such as a goblin, but a human of average intelligence would find it suspicious. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01428))_
- However, you can only make this resistance roll _once_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01429))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.10 How to Read Magic Details / 《 Ritual 》

- Magic of the **ritual** type can increase its effect (final score) due to carefully preparing and performing a ritual. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01431))_
- With these spells, you can add +1 to your final score for each day you perform the ritual. If additional casters who can use the same spell also participate in the ritual, you will gain +1 to your final score for each one. Even humans who cannot use spells can participate in the ritual. In this case, you can gain +1 to your final score for every 10 people (rounded down). However, the ritual procedures are very complicated, so those who have not been taught the procedure in advance will not be able to participate in the ritual. If it's ancient magic, the caster must have been taught at a school such as an _academy of sages_ , etc. and if it's holy (dark) magic, they must be a believer. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01432))_
- These bonuses are stacked in the form of _days x participants_ . For example, suppose a priest performs a _Remove Curse_ ritual. If the ritual takes two days (+2), one extra priest who can also use _Remove Curse_ participates (+1), and 30 believers participate (+3), the final score bonus will be _2 x (1 + 3) =_ _**+8**_ . _Fractions_ of the number of days must be _rounded down_ , so if you can't spend a _full_ day, the final score bonus will be _0_ , regardless of how many participants there are. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01433))_
- Unlike magic expansion, there is _no_ limit to the increase in final score through rituals. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01434))_
- A ritual must be performed without sleep or rest, and is usually limited to 2 days. If someone drops out during the ritual, their number will not be considered at all. In the previous example, if 10 believers drop out, even if it's right after the ritual begins, just before the ritual ends, or at any timing in between, the final score bonus will be _2 x (1 + 2) =_ _**+6**_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01435))_
- The person who makes the success roll is the one who takes the center role in performing the ritual. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01436))_
- If it's ancient magic, the caster must have been taught at a school such as an _academy of sages_ , etc. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01432))_
- Unlike magic expansion, there is _no_ limit to the increase in final score through rituals. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01434))_
- A ritual must be performed without sleep or rest, and is usually limited to 2 days. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01435))_
- In the previous example, if 10 believers drop out, even if it's right after the ritual begins, just before the ritual ends, or at any timing in between, the final score bonus will be _2 x (1 + 2) =_ _**+6**_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01435))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.10 How to Read Magic Details / 《 Lost 》

- Among ancient magic, there are some spells known only to a limited number of sorcerers, and spells that were lost with the fall of the ancient kingdom. These are called **lost spells** . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01439))_
- The game master gets to determine which spells are considered lost spells. It's acceptable to have _all_ spells on the magic list be lost, or conversely, to have all magic be _known_ and _no_ spells be lost. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01440))_
- If a spell says _lost_ under its magic details, it may be easier to maintain balance when enjoying the game if you consider it a lost spell. Unless the game master has a particular reason, please consider these to be lost spells. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01441))_
- Among ancient magic, there are some spells known only to a limited number of sorcerers, and spells that were lost with the fall of the ancient kingdom. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01439))_
- Unless the game master has a particular reason, please consider these to be lost spells. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01441))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.10 How to Read Magic Details / [Sample Magic Details]

- This spell allows the caster to understand how to read magic details. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01450))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill

- _High ancient_ are the great runes that were developed and studied during the time of the ancient kingdom. The power of these runes releases magic forces and brings about various effects. Many of the spells and runes of this system were lost with the fall of the ancient kingdom, but a small amount of them have been passed down to modern Forcelia, and are now referred to as **ancient magic** . The skill for using ancient magic is called the _sorcerer skill_ , and those who have this skill are called _sorcerers_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01478))_
- The skill for using ancient magic is called the _sorcerer skill_ , and those who have this skill are called _sorcerers_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01478))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Base Mental Power Cost 》

- The base mental power cost represents how much mental power is consumed when using that magic. As previously explained, this base mental power cost divided by the corresponding rune master skill level equals the actual mental power consumed by the caster. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01454))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Distance 》

- This represents the distance the magic can reach. Basically, magic works on things that the caster can see and are within this distance. Any exceptions will always be noted in the explanation that follows. If the distance is **touch** , the caster must touch the target with their hand or (for ancient magic) with their magical catalyst (see below). To cast these spells in combat, you must be _engaged_ with the target. At this time, there is no need to roll dice to determine whether you've touched your opponent, like with an attack hit check (you can touch them automatically). _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01456))_
- Basically, magic works on things that the caster can see and are within this distance. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01456))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Area 》

- This represents the target that the magic affects. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01458))_
- When it says **one** , it works on one enemy or ally. It is also possible for casters to cast it on themselves. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01460))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Duration 》

- This represents how long the magic will remain in effect. This includes **instant** , **18 rounds** , **1 day** , **permanent** , **until focus ends** or **until certain** **conditions are met** . For magic whose duration is _instant_ , the magic itself disappears in an instant, but its effects remain. Wounds caused by a _Fireball_ explosion will remain, and if you receive healing by _Cure Wounds_ , those wounds will be recovered instantly. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01463))_
- Wounds caused by a _Fireball_ explosion will remain, and if you receive healing by _Cure Wounds_ , those wounds will be recovered instantly. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01463))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Effect 》

- This is a brief description of the magic's effect. Once you've read the detailed description, you'll be able to recall the general effect of the magic just by looking at this. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01465))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Type 》

- Represents the type of magic. Please see 5.1.9: Magic Types. **Counters (negates):** and **counters (overpowers):** describe magic that can be negated _by_ this magic, while **countered (negated) by:** and **countered (overpowered) by:** describe magic that can negate _this_ magic. However, _Dispel Magic_ , _Counter Sense_ , _Suppress Elemental_ , _Dispel Order_ , _Rune Shield_ , _Perfect Cancellation_ , _Neutralize Elemental_ , and _Remove Curse_ omit this. Magic of the **mind** , **physical ability** , and **weapon enhancement** types also omit _counters_ and _countered by_ , since they are sufficiently described. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01467))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Resist 》

- This represents whether the magic can be resisted, and what will happen if it is resisted. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01471))_
- **None** : No resist can be performed. Spells always take their effect. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01472))_
- **Reduced Effect** : If resisted, the spell only takes an incomplete effect. Spells of the _damage_ type will have their strike power reduced by -10 and can no longer critical. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01474))_
- After these details are briefly written, a detailed description of each spell is written. Be sure to read it over before attempting to use something you've never used before. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01475))_
- After these details are briefly written, a detailed description of each spell is written. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01475))_

- If you don't obey these two things, you won't be able to use ancient magic. Other rules follow the basic rules of magic. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01483))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 High Ancient 》

- Sorcerers can speak, read, and write in high ancient. It seems that these runes were used in official texts and conversation in the ancient kingdom, but now much of it has been lost, except for the few that remain in spellbooks. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01488))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Low Ancient 》

- This was an everyday language of the ancient kingdom, called **low ancient** , and was the language used by citizens and slaves. Sorcerers can speak, read and write in this language. Low ancient was used in informal texts in the ancient kingdom. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01490))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Spellbook 》

- A sorcerer must somehow preserve the ancient magic spells they've learned. Otherwise, even those with the greatest minds cannot possibly memorize all the words, actions, etc. needed to cast spells. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01494))_
- For this reason, it is customary for sorcerers to write these spells down in a book called a **spellbook** . A spellbook is, so to speak, just a handwritten notebook, and the spellbook itself has no magical power of its own. However, because it's a very important thing, it would be a disaster if it were lost or stolen, so some sorcerers may keep several copies in reserve. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01495))_
- When you go on an adventure, or you're in a situation where you'd need to use magic, you'd usually bring your spellbook with you. However, no sorcerer looks at their spellbook every time they try to cast a spell. This is because the words and actions of a spell are usually sharply memorized in your head. A spellbook is used to review them, always confirming and ensuring your memory. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01496))_
- There are no special restrictions on spellbooks according to the rules. Nevertheless, keep in mind that sorcerers in Sword World always keep their spellbooks with them, and remember to take very good care of them. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01497))_
- However, because it's a very important thing, it would be a disaster if it were lost or stolen, so some sorcerers may keep several copies in reserve. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01495))_
- This is because the words and actions of a spell are usually sharply memorized in your head. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01496))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.11 Ancient Magic and the Sorcerer Skill / 《 Magical Catalyst 》

- Sorcerers require a special medium to cast spells. This is a **magical catalyst** , and it is through this that a sorcerer exercises the power of a spell. Usually, a specially-made mage's staff is used as a magical catalyst, made from a wooden staff with a _Create Device_ spell cast on it. This is why you must have a mage's staff as a restriction when using ancient magic. However, some sorcerers substitute other things besides staves. For example, Laverna, the witch of Orphan, uses an amethyst ring she wears on her right middle finger as her magical catalyst, and Cyanos, leader of the magic knights of Ramliearth, carries a small twig wand in his left hand as a magical catalyst. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01499))_
- For example, Laverna, the witch of Orphan, uses an amethyst ring she wears on her right middle finger as her magical catalyst, and Cyanos, leader of the magic knights of Ramliearth, carries a small twig wand in his left hand as a magical catalyst. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01499))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List

- This spell reflects magic cast on the caster directly back onto their opponent. If magic is cast on the person who casts this spell, that magic will rebound back to the opponent who cast it. At the same time, the effect of _Magic Reflection_ will disappear. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-02009))_
- However, this can only reflect magic which has an area of effect of _one_ . In the case of magic that affects a space, _Magic Reflection_ has no effect. Also, since the reflection is indiscriminate, even magic that’s _favorable_ towards the caster will be reflected. In addition, spells that nullify magic, such as _Dispel Magic_ , cannot be reflected. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-02011))_
- If a caster using _Magic Reflection_ casts other magic on his or herself, the effect of _Magic Reflection_ will be lost at the same time the new magic is cast. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-02012))_
- In addition, spells that nullify magic, such as _Dispel Magic_ , cannot be reflected. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-02011))_
- However, this can only reflect magic which has an area of effect of _one_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-02011))_

- This magic allows you to deal damage to monsters that cannot be damaged by normal weapons. However, in this case, the strike roll can only be made with the strike power set to 5, regardless of the weapon's own strike power. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01518))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / [ Sleep Cloud ]

- This spell alters the air in a space within a 5 meter radius from the target, creating a gas with the effect of instantly putting any creatures inside to sleep. Anything within the area is affected, friend or foe, but targets that make a successful resistance roll will be completely unaffected by the spell. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01537))_
- Those that fail to resist fall asleep, but since it’s a natural sleep, they will wake up immediately if there’s any noise, etc. in their surroundings. If there's combat, etc. happening in their surroundings, they can make a resistance roll each round, and wake up if successful. Also, if they're dealt physical or mental damage, if they receive a shock such as being hit or kicked even if it does not deal damage, or if an extremely loud noise is made, they will automatically wake up without the need for a resistance roll. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01538))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / [ Decrease Weight ]

- Distance=10 meters Area=One object Duration=18 rounds Effect=Reduce the weight of an object Type=Lost Counters (Negates): _Increase Weight_ Countered (Negated) By: _Increase Weight_ Expansion=Duration, distance, targets, effect (see description) Resist=None _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01550))_
- This spell is used on a single object and has the effect of reducing the target’s weight. If cast on a weapon or armor, it has the effect of reducing the target's required strength by -1 _without_ changing its strike power or defense power. When used on other objects, it has the ability to reduce their weight by about 90%. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01551))_
- This spell’s effect can be expanded. If you _double_ or _triple_ the amount of mental power you consume...... the required strength can become _-2_ or _-3_ ...... for weapons and armor. For other objects, it’ll be reduced by 10% each time. When reducing the weight of an object, it’s reduced by 90% each, the rate of _double_ expansion would be _0.9 x 0.9 = 0.81 times_ . For _triple_ , it’d be _0.9 x 0.9 x 0.9 = 0.721 times_ . To reduce the weight by _half_ , you must expand it _7 times_ , and to reduce it to _1/10th_ , you must expand it _22 times_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01552))_
- Even if you reduce the required strength, the strike power or defense power of weapons and armor will _not_ change. Also, in this case, required strength can only be reduced to 1. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01553))_
- Also, in this case, required strength can only be reduced to 1. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01553))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / [ Kindle ]

- This is a spell used on flammable objects several centimeters in size, causing them to ignite. The effect of the spell will disappear in an instant, but the object should burn on its own afterwards. This spell’s effect only works on highly flammable objects such as oil, dead grass, and sawdust, so it's completely useless if used on live trees or non-flammable materials. It has almost no effect on monsters either. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01572))_

This spell takes effect against anything that deals direct damage, whether it's a physical attack or a magical attack. However, it has no effect at all on spells that are offensive but do not deal damage to life force. It also cannot prevent damage dealt to mental power _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01580))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / Duration=Permanent

- This spell has the effect of giving magic resistance to objects that do not have it. If the targeted object is exposed to another spell that's not _detection_ type, it will resist that spell unless the opponent succeeds on a success roll against a target score equal to the final score from when _Magic Protection_ was cast. If a successful resist, the opponent’s spell will either completely lose its effect, or will take only an incomplete effect. If the resist fails, the spell will take its full effect, and furthermore the _Magic Protection_ spell itself will be removed. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01589))_
- Even spells with a _resist_ of _none_ can be resisted by _Magic Protection_ . In this case, the spell will take no effect at all. For example, if you cast _Kindle_ on a bundle of straw that has _Magic Protection_ cast on it, if _Kindle_ cannot break through the protection of _Magic Protection_ (the final score is insufficient), it won't be able to ignite. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01590))_
- This spell is powerless against spells that belong to _detection_ . Therefore, objects with this spell cast on them _will_ respond to _Sense Magic_ . _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01591))_
- Also, if you cast it on something that naturally has resistance (humans, fae, youma, etc.), it will have no effect at all. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01592))_
- If the targeted object is exposed to another spell that's not _detection_ type, it will resist that spell unless the opponent succeeds on a success roll against a target score equal to the final score from when _Magic Protection_ was cast. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01589))_
- For example, if you cast _Kindle_ on a bundle of straw that has _Magic Protection_ cast on it, if _Kindle_ cannot break through the protection of _Magic Protection_ (the final score is insufficient), it won't be able to ignite. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01590))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / [ Light ]

- This spell is used on an object or a point in space. It has no effect at all when used on living things. Using a single point as a light source, a space with a 10 meter radius is filled with white magical light. The further away you are from the light source, the more the effect of the light will fade. If you cast it on a portable object such as a shield, you can move the light source along with the object. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01602))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / Distance=Touch

- Effect=Puts a magical lock on objects that open and close, such as doors, lids, etc. Type=Target score Countered (Overpowered) By: _Unlock_ Expansion=Final score, duration Resist=None _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01607))_
- This spell can be used on objects that open and close, such as doors, treasure chest lids, etc. to place a magical lock on them. As a result, the door or lid will never open unless you chant the password you chose when casting the spell. This password does _not_ have to be in high ancient. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01608))_
- This spell can be used on objects that open and close, such as doors, treasure chest lids, etc. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01608))_

### Chapter 5: Magic / 5.1.12 Ancient Magic List / [ Oak ]

- This spell creates a 1-meter tall, goblin-esque wood golem from a tree branch. This simplified version of a wood golem came to be called an _Oak_ because the material used was many oak tree branches, so that eventually became the name of the spell. Oaks can only fight, and the caster must specify whom to attack. Or otherwise, they can specify a location, and have the oak attack anyone invading that location. After the spell's duration expires, the oak will turn back into a branch. _(Sword World RPG - Complete Edition.pdf (source-range-870a16bc-01612))_
